LOCATION: ALEXANDRIA
==================================================

About Alexandria
Alexandria Governorate is one of the beautiful seaside living destinations in Egypt. It boasts many ancient and modern landmarks across the country, as well as various recreational and educational facilities.
Alexandria covers 2818.77 km² of total land area in Egypt, overlooking the beautiful Mediterranean Sea. Its pristine coastline extends over 70 km.
Being one of the top seaside urban areas, many of the top residential gated communities are situated in the Alexandria Governorate.
Various real estate tycoons built state-of-the-art compounds in Alexandria, including Palm Hills Developments. In addition to being a one-of-a-kind residential area, Alexandria Governorate has long been a favorite vacation destination for Egyptians.
Alexandria Egypt Location
Alexandria Governorate location in Egypt, offers its residents and those looking forward to a refreshing vacation the utmost convenience. First thing to know is that it is situated in the northwest of the Delta.
It is bordered by the Mediterranean Sea from the north, El Beheira Governorate from the east, and Matrouh Governorate from the west. In fact, the Alexandria, Egypt, strategic location makes the governorate approximately:
50 km away from Borg El Arab Airport
55 km away to
North Coast
120 km away to
New Alamein City
345 km away to
Ain Sokhna

International Coastal Road (also known as Alexandria-Marsa Matrouh Road)

Alexandria Map & Neighborhoods
Alexandria Governorate is the second-largest city in Egypt in terms of population. It is divided into various neighborhoods, boasting a wide variety of residential and mixed-use properties.
Administratively, the governorate is divided into three main cities: Alexandria City, the capital of the governorate, Borg Al Arab, and New Borg Al Arab.
Each district has its own vibe, aesthetic, and reasons that make it a unique living destination.

Things to Do in Alexandria
There are boundless things to do in Alexandria Governorate. It is filled with bewitching destinations, whether you are looking forward to some leisurely time or wandering down a historical lane.
Many of the historic landmarks in Egypt are situated in Alexandria. For instance, the city exhibits:
The Catacombs of Kom el Shoqafa, which is one of the Middle Ages’ seven wonders.
Montaza Palace, which was the summer palace of Mohamed Ali till King Farouk.
The Alexandria National Museum narrates the history of Egypt through different ages and historical periods.
Qaitbay Citadel and its meticulous blend of architectural styles.
The Lighthouse of Alexandria is one of the seven wonders of the world.
The Graeco-Roman Museum, one of Alexandria’s archeological museums, boasts a wide range of coins from different countries.
If you are an art lover or a bibliophile, Alexandria Governorate is the home of many exceptional art galleries, libraries, artspaces, and bookstores, such as:
Alexandria Bibliotheca
Egyptian American Book Center

Bayt Al Kotob

Vermilion Gallery
Furthermore, there are a number of must-visit destinations in Alexandria Governorate, including:
Royal Jewelry Museum
Cavofy Museum
The Archaeological Museum in the Library of Alexandria
Deir Mar Mina (St. Mina Monastery), the largest Coptic monastery in Egypt
Aquarium Museum, if you are interested in marine creatures

Alexandria History
Throughout the Ptolemies, Romans, and until the Arab conquest in 640 AD, the Alexandria Governorate was the capital of Egypt. Taking it back to the very beginning, the city was founded by Alexander the Great, specifically in 322 BC.
Alexander the Great was riding along the Mediterranean Sea coast when the area between the coastline and Lake Mariout took him by awe. It was a flawless destination to establish a new city, with easy access to fresh water from the Nile.
Alexander the Great turned the Alexandria Governorate into a one-of-a-kind area, with the brilliance of Denocrates. He was one of Alexander’s close advisors, and he chose to build the city with a hippo-damme theme.
This aesthetic was popular in Greek cities back in the 5th Century B.C. Alexandria City was divided into five quarters, which are:
Royal Quarter
Jewish Quarter
Canopus Street (known now as Fouad Street)
Sedra
Nabi Daniel Street
Alexandria has remained a state-of-the-art cosmopolitan city throughout the years. But during the 16th Century, it went through a period of decline because of epidemics. It returned to its prosperity in the 19th Century, becoming well-known for its ambivalent heritage.
Furthermore, Alexandria witnessed many of the events that happened during World War I (from 1914 to 1918) and the 1919 revolution in Egypt. Marches and demonstrations started from the Mosque of Abil Abbas El Morsy towards the Municipality’s old building in Alexandria.

LOCATION: 6TH-SETTLEMENT

About 6th settlement
6th Settlement is one of the elite neighborhoods in New Cairo City. It has been formerly called “Al Aml Triangle” and its name has been changed since it is located at the endpoint of 5th Settlement.
The New Urban Communities Authority is in charge of developing this area under the supervision of the Ministry of Housing, Utilities, and Urban Communities, and it works closely with New Cairo’s Development Authority.
New Cairo’s 6th Settlement is one of the most recent upscale residential areas, offering a premium location and many opulent compounds. The area stands out as a residential, administrative, and commercial extension of New Cairo City.
6th Settlement New Cairo Egypt, extends over 4800 acres (20 million square meters) of land to the east of Cairo. Also, it is privileged with the prime location that makes it easily accessible from all the major roads.
6th Settlement Location In New Cairo
6th Settlement enjoys a prime location in New Cairo, Egypt, which is within close proximity to all major highways and destinations. This central location of the district was perfectly picked and planned so that it would be an easily accessible gateway for residents and investors.
6th Settlement New Cairo, Egypt, is found at the
endpoint
of Fifth Settlement, on the road that is between Ain Sokhna Road and Middle Ring Road, and very close to the New Administrative Capital. It is exactly found on the southern side of Ain Sokhna-Kattameya Road.
Also, it is planned that the South 90 axis and street would be the main administrative, commercial, and connection axis for this new area. Thanks to its ideal central location, 6th Settlement is:
30 minutes away from
New Capital City
32 minutes away from 1st, 3rd,and 5th Settlements in New Cairo
40 minutes away from Cairo International Airport
60 minutes away from
Ain Sokhna
Within close proximity to Nasr City, Heliopolis, Maadi, South 90 Street, and AUC

About Northern Expansion
Northern Expansions is one of the elite residential areas in 6th of October City, west of Cairo. It boasts a wide range of luxurious real estate developments, beautifully landscaped open spaces, and top-quality infrastructure.
One of the reasons why the area is a top choice for a residential destination is its prime location in October City. It is in proximity to many of the area’s shopping centres, renowned universities & schools, and high-end hospitals.
In fact, Northern Expansions is around 10 minutes away from El Hossary, and its prime location can be accessed through several main roads, such as Al Wahat Road and 26th of July Mehwar.

LOCATION: EL-GOUNA

About El Gouna
Samih Sawiris, the visionary mind behind Orascom Development, stumbled upon El Gouna in the late 80s and conceived it as a one-of-a-kind sustainable paradise on the alluring Red Sea coast.
He thought such a natural Eden could be a true testament to the notion of “Life as it should be”, when it turns into a fully integrated resort town.
Orascom Development started creating Gouna in 1989, turning such a haven in Hurghada into a thriving community by being committed to building an eco-friendly development with state-of-the-art architecture and boundless facilities.
Since then, it has flourished to become a vibrant, worldwide living and vacation destination in Hurghada, Egypt. It is known not only for its pristine beaches but also for its luxurious resorts and neighborhoods, its exquisite offerings, and its artistic and cultural scene.
El Gouna Location
Gouna is one of the most scenic destinations in Egypt, overlooking the beautiful Red Sea, and close to
Hurghada
. It is only a 4-hour flight from Europe’s major capitals.
The prime location of Gouna on the Red Sea coastline made the area easily accessible via various transportation routes, from buses to airplanes.
There are over 60 daily flights to Gouna, from Western and Eastern Europe to Russia and the Middle East.
Distance from Cairo to Gouna
El Gouna is approximately 445 km away from Cairo, around a 5-hour drive. It can be reached by car or bus through Hurghada - Al Ismaileya/ Hurghada - Cairo/ Route 65M.
Moreover, you can travel to Gouna from Cairo with approximately 4-hour flights.
Distance from Hurghada to El Gouna, Egypt
The ideal location of Gouna, Egypt, puts it 25 km north of Hurghada. It can be reached within 33 minutes via:
Hurghada - Al Ismaileya Road
Hurghada - Cairo Road
Moreover, it is in proximity to Hurghada International Airport, around 40 km away.
Key Roads in El-Gouna
Several major highways and axes are in proximity to or pass through El-Gouna, making commuting to the beachtown a breeze. They include:
Hurghada - Ismailia Road
Hurghada - Cairo Highway
Gouna - Hurghada Road
El Gouna Egypt Map
When Orascom Development initiated the construction process of Gouna in Egypt, it began by creating enchanting lagoons and world-class hotels. Afterward, the expansion of state-of-the-art golf courses started. That’s how the story of the town began on the Red Sea shores.
El Gouna, Hurghada, became a fully sufficient town, which was built to offer its visitors and residents a high-quality experience that is all about sustainability and culture. Its map outlines a broad array of neighborhoods, fancy resorts, distinguishing facilities, and more.
Gouna is stretched across 10 km of azure shoreline on the dazzling Red Sea coast. It is a self-contained community that features a wide range of essential and recreational facilities, such as:

In partnership with Orascom Development, Gouna Film Festival (GFF) is one of the most artistic festivals in the MENA region. It is held to showcase how films depict cultural diversity, support emerging filmmakers, and offer them networking opportunities.

About North Coast-Sahel
Situated on the Mediterranean Sea coastline, North Coast, Egypt, is one of the favorite vacation destinations during summer. It is famous for its pristine beaches, distinctive amenities, luxurious resorts, vibrant nightlife, and boundless leisure activities.
El Sahel stretches from Alexandria to Marsa Matrouh. This Mediterranean Eden is a one-of-a-kind escapade from the city, where vacationers can unwind, relax, and revive their bodies and minds.
North Coast in Egypt is well-known for its elite resorts with a broad array of beach houses and high-end amenities, which ensure the visitors and homeowners’ utmost hassle-free coastal experience.
North Coast Location
North Coast is situated between Alexandria and Marsa Matrouh Governorate. It is around 30 minutes away from Alexandria via the International Coastal Road.
Several main roads pass through El Sahel, making it easily accessible from many destinations in Egypt.
Moreover, you can reach it by plane; there are several airports nearby, such as:
Borg El Arab International Airport
Marsa Matrouh International Airport
Key Roads in North Coast, Egypt
Several main roads pass through North Coast Sahel in Egypt, and they are:
International Coastal Road (Alexandria - Marsa Matrouh Road)
Wadi El Natroun Road
Dabaa Road
Distance From Cairo to North Coast Sahel
Reaching North Coast from anywhere in Cairo is convenient, and it is around 2 hours and a half hours away from the city.
Keep in mind that the North Coast extends across a large area, so the time varies depending on your destination and your pickup point.

LOCATION: EL-SHOROUK
==================================================

About El Shorouk
El Shorouk City is one of the third-generation cities in the east of Cairo that was established by the presidential decree (325/1995). It is part of the Cairo Governorate and occupies 16.11 thousand acres.
Of this land area, 9,200 acres have been dedicated to urban development and facilities, leaving the remaining space for roads, green areas, and other services.
Because of its careful design, Al Shorouk will continue to be among Egypt's greenest cities. It is administered by the New Urban Communities Authority of Egypt, which has built many educational facilities, hospitals and health centers, commercial centers, and sports centers.
The city is unique in that it is 250 meters above sea level, which has a good impact on the weather. It’s pleasant in both summers and winters.
El Shorouk City Location
El Shorouk City is located on the Cairo - Ismailia Desert Road, Kilo 37. Going down this road, you would get to the city on the eastern side after passing
Al Rehab Compound
and New Heliopolis.
Thanks to this location, El Shorouk City Cairo, is:
5 km away from Madinaty Compound and Al-Rehab
Bordered from the east by Badr City and New Heliopolis
In very close proximity to
New Administrative City
Key Roads in Al Shorouk Egypt
The main roads in El Shorouk City Cairo, include:
Cairo - Suez Desert Road
Cairo - Ismailia Road
Sadat Road
Gamal Abdel Nasser Road
Orabi Road
Qingnian Road
Oasis Road
El Shorouk City Map & Districts
Covering
16.11 thousand acres
of land, El Shorouk City has a smartly designed map that is divided into several districts. They include:
First District
The First District is also called The Villas Neighborhood. It is situated between the Ismailia Desert Road and the city center.
It hosts numerous important educational and service landmarks, including Dover International School and Mina Language School, as well as shopping centers, including Galaxy Mall, University Mall, and Carrefour.
Seventh District
The Seventh District is the most well-known and affordable residential area in El Shorouk and is situated in the heart of the city, making it an excellent strategic location.
In addition to the numerous open spaces amidst the buildings, the neighborhood is renowned for its wide streets and highways. There are several striking city monuments in the region as well. It features the Arab League, Lebanese University, and French University.
Eighth District
The Eighth District in El Shorouk City is an excellent area to walk or ride a bicycle because its roadways are bordered with lovely trees. It is also home to an Al Shorouk Club and Banque Misr branch.
Al Nakheel District
Al Nakheel District is one of the city's most well-liked neighborhoods because of the El Shorouk complexes. Situated on the western route that leads into the city, it is renowned for its elegance and tranquility.
The British University, El Shorouk Academy, and some of the most opulent El Shorouk compounds are located there.

About New Zayed
New Zayed City is one of the most recently built high-end residential areas. It is considered the western geographical extension of El Sheikh Zayed City. The new city spans a land area of 21,000 acres, with its first phase taking up 8000 of those acres.
Thanks to being a luxurious area and to its inclusion and offering high-end facilities, New Zayed City became very popular and a resident-attractive city. The city enjoys a very strategic, connecting location to Zayed that opens it up to the city’s main facilities.

New Zayed City in Egypt enjoys a prime location that is easily accessible from major destinations and roads.
The first question that pops to mind when talking about New Zayed's location is whether it is in Giza Governorate or Cairo Governorate, and the answer to this question is that, like October and Zayed cities, is located in Giza Governorate.

In the First District of El Sheikh Zayed
4 km (a 2-minute ride) from Zayed City

LOCATION: AL-DABAA
==================================================

About Al Dabaa
El Dabaa is a town in Matrouh situated along the northwest coast of Egypt. It lies approximately 160 kilometers from Alexandria and about 140 kilometers from Marsa Matrouh, which serves as the capital of the Matrouh Governorate.
This area is well known for its beautiful coastal scenery and is a popular region for vacationers who want to spend a memorable summer time by the Mediterranean Coast.
El Dabaa is also filled with key facilities making vacationers enjoy a comfortable and convenient time.
Dabaa North Coast Egypt​ Location
El Dabaa is a prominent town situated in the Matrouh Governorate of Egypt, nestled between the scenic areas of
Ras Al Hikma
and
Sidi Abdelrahman
. Its strategic location along the North Coast offers convenient access to several key cities.
Al Dabaa Egypt approximately 170 kilometers from Alexandria, which translates to a drive time of about an hour and a half.
The distance between El Dabaa Egypt and Cairo is around 340 kilometers, requiring an estimated 4-hour drive.
For those heading from New Alamein, El Dabaa is just 73 kilometers away, taking roughly 55 minutes.
El Dabaa North Coast location is also about 128 kilometers from Marsa Matrouh, which can be reached in about 1 hour.
El Dabaa North Coast is near Borg El Arab International Airport, Andalusia Hospital in the North Coast, and Rixsol Hotel.
People can conveniently access Dabaa Marsa Matrouh​ via the Alexandria - Marsa Matrouh Road (
International Coastal Road
), making it an easily reachable destination for both residents and visitors alike.
Al Dabaa Roads
El Dabaa on the North Coast of Egypt boasts a well-developed network of main roads that facilitate easy commuting and enhance accessibility to the area. Among the key routes are:
International Coastal Road (also known as Alexandria - Marsa Matrouh Coastal Road), which runs along the coastline, provides direct access to various coastal destinations and resorts.
Al Dabaa Egypt Road, which serves as a crucial link for local traffic and connects El Dabaa to surrounding regions.
These roads not only streamline transportation but also contribute to the area's appeal as a desirable location for residents, tourists, and investors alike.
The efficient road network supports the growth of the community and encourages economic development by making it easier for people to commute to and from El Dabaa.
El Dabaa Compounds & Resorts
El Dabaa is home to a diverse array of upscale resorts that offer visitors a distinctive vacation experience, boated by luxury, stunning views, and comfort. Among the notable compounds and resorts in the El Dabaa North Coast are:
D.O.S.E North Coast
Developed by the real estate developer, Akam Alrajhi Developments. The resort is located in the 174th km of the North Coast, specifically in the Dabaa area. D.O.S.E North Coast has a wide array of facilities and lavish beach houses making it the perfect place for spending a memorable vacation.
Seazen North Coast
Seazen is a high-end resort developed by the real estate guru, Al Qamzi Developments. Al Dabaa Egypt has a massive area of 204 acres with the majority of the total area dedicated to the landscapes, amenities, and water features.
Waterway North Coast
The Waterway North Coast is a premier development that is transforming the concept of beachfront living. Developed by Waterway Developments, this expansive resort spans 124 acres and is strategically located at the 173rd kilometer of the Alexandria - Marsa Matrouh Road.
With its luxurious amenities and picturesque surroundings, the Water Way North Coast Resort is poised to provide an unparalleled vacation experience, making it a sought-after destination for those looking to enjoy the beauty of the North Coast while indulging in a lifestyle of comfort and sophistication.
SouthMed City
SouthMed City, developed by the esteemed Talaat Moustafa Group (TMG), is a comprehensive coastal destination located in Al Dabaa on the North Coast.
Spanning an impressive 23 million square meters, South Med TMG is designed to provide residents and visitors with an abundance of world-class amenities and activities, all set against the stunning backdrop of the Mediterranean Sea.
La Vista Bay East
La Vista Bay East is a remarkable resort developed by La Vista Developments, known for its sophisticated and elegant architecture that embodies the La Vista Development's core values of luxury, comfort, and exclusivity.
Situated in the heart of the North Coast at the 152 km mark on the Alexandria - Marsa Matrouh Road, La Vista Bay East El Dabaa is strategically positioned to take advantage of the area's natural beauty. This coveted destination spans an impressive 1,200,000 square meters.
D-Bay North Coast
D-Bay is a lavish resort developed by the real estate shining star, Tatweer Misr across 200 acres of land in Dabaa. The resort is filled to the brim with endless amenities and luxury beach houses making it an ideal resort for spending a memorable vacation. Tatweer Misr partnered with Gianluca Peluffo & Partners which is an Italian architectural firm to design the D-Bay North Coast Project.
These El Dabaa Compounds and resorts not only enhance the allure of El Dabaa as a vacation destination but also cater to a variety of preferences, ensuring that every vacationer can find the perfect setting for relaxation and enjoyment.
El Dabaa Egypt Map
El Dabaa is situated 300 kilometers (approximately 184 miles) from Cairo, along the northern coast of Egypt.
The Ministry of Housing reviewed the status of land development projects under the jurisdiction of the New Urban Communities Authority in the West Dabaa area, encompassing an area of around 1,230 acres.
A comprehensive urban community is set to be established, complete with essential infrastructure, aimed at accommodating the residents of both the coastal and inland regions of West Dabaa.
Additionally, there will be the creation of service areas for the local population and regional investment zones overlooking the coastal road.
The minister also presented an update on the land allocation, the planning specifics for the area, and the situation regarding the investment zone. Bear in mind that El Dabaa North Coast includes many facilities for its residents.
Al-Dabaa Facilities
El Dabaa on the North Coast of Egypt is equipped with a variety of key facilities that significantly enhance daily living for residents. These facilities include:
Hypermarkets
: Offering a wide range of shopping options, these hypermarkets cater to the daily needs of residents, making grocery shopping convenient and accessible.
Hospital and Medical Centers
: Essential for healthcare, these facilities ensure that residents have access to medical services and emergency care when needed.

Banks and ATMs
: Financial services are readily available, allowing residents to manage their finances easily and securely.
Transportation
: Efficient transportation options facilitate easy commuting within El Dabaa and to nearby cities, enhancing connectivity for residents.
These facilities contribute to making El Dabaa a well-rounded community, ensuring that residents have access to essential services and amenities that support a comfortable and convenient lifestyle.
North Coast Egypt
North Coast Egypt (Sahel), situated along the Mediterranean Sea, is a premier vacation destination, especially during the summer months. Known for its pristine beaches and luxurious resorts, it offers a perfect escape for those looking to unwind and rejuvenate.
The
North Coast
is well-known for its clear turquoise waters and powdery white sands, providing an idyllic setting for relaxation and leisure activities. Visitors can enjoy sunbathing, swimming, and various water sports in a stunning natural environment.
North Coast includes various areas which are:
Ras El Hekma
: Stretched from the 178th kilo to the 220th kilo of the International Coastal Road. It’s one of the most famous areas in the North Coast.
Sidi Abdelrahman
: Stretches from the 124th KM to the 144th KM, offering a beautiful expanse of coastline that is popular for its luxurious resorts and pristine beaches.
El Alamein
: El Alamein City is a stunning coastal city in Egypt that overlooks the Mediterranean Sea. Spanning an impressive 48,917 acres of land between the Alexandria and Matrouh Governorates, it extends more than 60 km south of the coastal strip, making it a significant area both geographically and culturally.
Sidi Heneish: Sidi Henish is ideally situated on the North Coast extending from the 221st kilo to the 250th kilo of the International Coastal Road.

The city was called El Alamein because it is situated between two mountains: Gabal Al Malh and Gabal Al Tair. The borders of El Alamein City in Egypt extend from Wadi El Natroun to El Dabaa. Its population is estimated to be more than
10,000 people
.

El Sokhna is the perfect place to escape the hustle and bustle of the city, and it is approximately an hour’s drive from Cairo. In addition to having one of the most stunning coastlines in the world, the city boasts many upscale resorts and amenities.
Ain Sokhna is known for its refreshing summer and winter, as well as a perfect place for a weekend getaway.

Galala City in Ain El Sokhna
One of the most popular destinations in Ain El Sokhna is Galala City. It is composed of several mountains, spaced 1200 meters apart. They are 700 meters above sea level, and they have a picturesque view.

Ain Sokhna Port & Industrial Zone
One of the most important industrial hubs in Egypt is Ain Sokhna Port & Industrial Zone. It is considered a major industrial and logistical center, and it is situated at the southern entrance to the Suez Canal.
Ain Sokhna Port and Industrial Zone features residential and commercial districts, paved roads, railroads, and port facilities. It also connects Suez and Cairo to the town. Moreover, it has shipbuilding, ship transportation, ship refueling, container recycling, and repair services.
Finally, the Ain Sokhna Port and Industrial Zone occupies 22.3 km² of the city’s total land area.

Ain Sokhna Facilities
Ain Sukhna Egypt
is a fully-fledged entertainment, medical, commercial, and educational hub, with a wide range of facilities. The town exhibits:
Sulfur Springs
Ain Al Sokhna's name was inspired by its close proximity to hot sulfur springs that originate from Ataqa Mountain in the northern part of Egypt's Eastern Desert. This is equivalent to "Hot Springs" in English.
One of Ain Sokhna's unique tourist attractions is the sulfur springs, which many Arab and international visitors come to in order to cure a variety of illnesses, such as joint pain and skin diseases.
Sandy Beaches
Ain Sokhna’s pristine beaches are a perfect destination for water sports like swimming, snorkeling, windsurfing, surfing, diving, underwater photography, and mountaineering, as well as for beautiful views from above and observing coral reefs and quiet bays in the deep sea.
Some of the beaches in Ain Sokhna are Compost Beach, Petroleum Beach, Mina Oasis Beach, and Sadat Beach.
Moreover, Ain Sokhna exhibits:
Many commercial centers from which you can get all your needs.
Various world-class hotels.
Top-notch restaurants.
Numerous aqua parks.

Ain Sokhna Weather
With an average temperature of 29°C (83°F), July is the hottest month in El Ein Sokhna. January is the coldest, with 14°C (57°F).
July also has the most sunlight hours, with 13 per day. The winters in Ain Sukhna are cold, dry, and primarily clear, while the summers are lengthy, hot, humid, arid, and clear.
The average annual temperature fluctuates between 11°C (52°F) and 33°C (92°F), and it is rarely lower or higher than 7°C (46°F) or 36°C (97°F).
Mid-May through late October is the ideal time of year to visit Ain Sukhna for hot-weather activities, according to the beach/pool score.
In a nutshell, the weather of Ain Sokhna makes it a year-round destination.

LOCATION: HURGHADA

About Hurghada
Hurghada, Egypt, derives its name from a well-known plant that grows in the region. This vibrant city has become one of the most prominent tourist destinations along the stunning shores of the Red Sea. It is also a fully equipped beachtown to live in.
Hurghada is ideally located in southern Egypt, and it stretches along 40 km of coastline dominated by various types of tourist facilities.
Over the past few decades, it has undergone significant development, evolving from its humble origins into a bustling hub for travelers seeking sun, sea, and adventure.
Visitors are now treated to a diverse array of activities, from snorkeling and diving in the vibrant coral reefs to enjoying the local cuisine.
The town attracts not only Egyptian tourists from Cairo, the Delta, and Upper Egypt but also travelers from Europe and other regions around the world. This diverse mix of visitors contributes to the vibrant atmosphere and cultural exchange in the area.
It’s also worth noting that this city is a place where people can purchase a house by the beach and live a comfortable lifestyle, as it’s filled with key facilities, from medical to educational facilities.
Hurghada Egypt Location
One of the most popular questions is “Where is Hurghada, Egypt, located?” and the answer is it is situated on the Red Sea coast.
Hurghada is easily reachable via Hurghada International Airport, which serves as a major gateway for travelers and residents. The airport is located just a short distance from the city center, facilitating convenient travel for tourists arriving from various parts of the world.
Additionally, the city is connected by road to other popular destinations along the Red Sea. The Hurghada, Egypt, location is approximately:
455 kilometers from Cairo via the Hurghada - Al Ismaileya/Hurghada - Cairo Road. This distance can vary slightly depending on the specific route taken.
1 hour away from Cairo to Hurghada by plane.
816 km away from Sharm El Sheikh.
32 KM away from El Gouna.
Key Roads in Hurghada, Egypt
Several major roads and highways pass through Hurghada, making commuting to the city a breeze. The beachtown is easily accessible via:
Hurghada - Safaga Road
Hurghada - El Quseir Road
Ras Gharib Road
Hurghada - Cairo Road
Distance from Cairo to Hurghada
The distance from Cairo to Hurghada is approximately 460 kilometers (about 287 miles). Travelers can expect the trip to take around 5 to 6 hours by car or bus. The duration can vary based on several factors, including traffic conditions, time of day, and the chosen route.
Alternatively, a flight from Cairo to Hurghada is much quicker, taking about 1 hour. This makes it convenient for both local and international tourists to access the beautiful coastal city.
Hurghada Egypt Map
The Hurghada map reveals a variety of distinct areas, each with its own unique character and charm.
Whether tourists or residents are looking to immerse themselves in local culture, experience modern amenities, or relax by the marina and enjoy the beautiful waters, Hurghada has something to offer for every vacationer.
It beautifully blends the old with the new and features some of the top hotel chains on Villages Road, as well as in nearby tourist areas like Sahl Hasheesh and El Gouna to the south.
The city is accessible via Hurghada International Airport, which offers direct flights to various cities in Europe. It has various upscale resorts and neighborhoods, where tourists can enjoy one-of-a-kind vacations.
Downtown Hurghada
To the north of Hurghada lies the historic El Dahar. It’s known for its maze of narrow streets, traditional souks, and a charming Christian Coptic Church. This area is home to the recently restored mosque and the Old Harbour, which leads to the new marina.
The marina features an exclusive selection of shops and excellent dining options, making it a popular spot for both locals and tourists.
It’s worth noting that the bustling souks (markets) in this area are filled with vibrant colors and enticing aromas, offering everything from spices to handcrafted goods.
To the south, there’s El Memsha, the main resort area of Hurghada. This area is characterized by modern hotels that line the coastal road, providing visitors with easy access to the beach and various amenities.
El Memsha is perfect for those looking to enjoy a luxurious vacation experience while being close to the vibrant life of the city.
For those in search of the most renowned thoroughfare in Hurghada, the main street in Downtown Hurghada, or its city center, is Sheraton Road.
Sheraton Street stands out as a vibrant street, and it is well-known for a multitude of shops and restaurants, making it a bustling hub for both locals and visitors.
Additionally, it is conveniently located near numerous hotels and resorts along the beach, enhancing its appeal as a central point for leisure and commerce.
Mamsha Hurghada
Mamsha Hurghada, also known as the Touristic Promenade, showcases the city’s dedication to offering an exceptional tourist experience.
This stunning 7-kilometer waterfront promenade beautifully combines luxury with both local and international hospitality. Visitors can enjoy a variety of iconic commercial brands, making it a vibrant destination for shopping, dining, and leisurely strolls along the coast.

ideally situated on the eastern shores of Egypt, overlooking the stunning Red Sea coast. Its location is easily accessible and conveniently close to Hurghada. Travelers can reach Soma Bay comfortably from anywhere in Egypt by bus, car, or plane.

Soma Bay

Sahl Hasheesh in Hurghada Red Sea Governorate
Sahl Hasheesh
is a stunning neighborhood located along the Red Sea coast of Egypt, situated approximately 18 kilometers south of Hurghada International Airport.
This picturesque area is renowned for its breathtaking natural beauty, featuring a series of islands and vibrant coral reefs that make it a prime destination for both diving and snorkeling enthusiasts.
El Gouna
Al Gouna, Egypt
, is a modern and world-class neighborhood situated along Egypt's stunning Red Sea coast, just a short distance from Hurghada.
This picturesque destination is uniquely designed and built along the shoreline and on small islands, creating a beautiful landscape, coral reefs, and sandy beaches. At the heart of El Gouna lies the lively Abu Tig Marina, a vibrant area lined with an array of restaurants and bars.
This marina serves as a social hub where visitors can enjoy a meal with a view of the yachts or unwind with a drink as the sun sets over the water. The atmosphere is lively, making it a perfect spot for both relaxation and socializing.
Al Sakkala In Hurghada
Al Sakkala is another prominent area in Hurghada, known for its modern amenities and vibrant atmosphere. This neighborhood is home to many hotels, restaurants, and shops, making it a popular choice for tourists.
The beachfront promenade in Al Sakkala offers stunning views of the Red Sea and is lined with cafes and bars, providing a lively spot for relaxation and socializing. This area is ideal for visitors who want to be close to the action while enjoying a more contemporary resort experience.
Hurghada's neighborhoods each offer a unique perspective on the city, from the traditional charm of El Dahar to the modern vibrancy of AlGouna, Al Sakkala, and the tranquility of Sahl Hasheesh.
Makadi Bay
Makadi Bay
is a picturesque resort town situated on the western coast of the Red Sea, approximately 30 kilometers south of Hurghada.
Nestled between serene desert landscapes, sand dunes, and the Red Sea mountains, this idyllic destination boasts long stretches of soft white sand and crystal-clear waters. The inshore reefs are home to a vibrant array of marine life, making them a paradise for snorkeling and diving enthusiasts.
Within the area, Makadi Mall offers a diverse selection of dining options, featuring a la carte restaurants serving Egyptian, Indian, Chinese, Italian, and French cuisine.

Things to Do in Hurghada

Practice kite surfing at El Gouna: Try your hand at kite surfing in El Gouna, known for its ideal wind conditions and beautiful lagoons.

About New Cairo
New Cairo City is one of the top living and hangout destinations in Egypt, in Cairo Governorate. It sprawls over 85,000 acres of land in East Cairo, featuring some of the finest facilities and high-end services.
Well-known for its luxurious real estate developments, the city is one of the most tranquil residential destinations in Cairo Governorate, where its homeowners can enjoy the perks of urban living with serene vibes.
Moreover, New Cairo is divided into several neighborhoods, each with its own characteristics and distinguishing details. It features a broad array of premium facilities, from high-end universities and schools to medical facilities, shopping malls, and vast recreational destinations.
New Cairo City Location
New Cairo City is ideally situated between Heliopolis and El Maadi, two of the top residential areas in Cairo Governorate. It can easily be reached from many areas in Cairo, thanks to its good transportation network.

LOCATION: OLD-CAIRO

About Old Cairo
What is old cairo?
Old Cairo Egypt, or Masr al-Qadima in Arabic, is among the most popular neighborhoods in Egypt that has a history and heritage. The area is not just a mere residential district; rather, it is a neighborhood full of life, stories, rituals, and monuments in every corner.
The area has been listed on UNESCO's World Heritage List since 1979 for its historical value. Also, this mystical neighborhood is known by UNESCO as “Historical Cairo”, sometimes it is also called “Fatimid Cairo”, and “Old Coptic Cairo”.
These names reflect the essence of the area, as the historical name, which is one of the oldest historical districts in Cairo. Moreover, it is known as Fatimid Cairo because it was the center of the Fatimid Dynasty in Egypt, and most caliphs laid out the area’s streets and gave them their names.
Lastly, it's Coptic because it currently holds most of the old Coptic monuments and churches in Cairo. Old Cairo City, Egypt, is an exceptional gateway for tourists, homeowners, investors, and history lovers.
From lavish compounds to premium facilities and unique historical monuments, Old Cairo, Egypt, offers an exceptional destination to live, invest in, and marvel at Egyptian history.
Old Cairo Location​
Old City Cairo
Egypt, is found on the eastern bank of the Nile River in the Southern district of Cairo Governorate.
The area is bordered by the Cairo Aqueduct (Sur Megra El-Ayoun) from the north and the Ring Road from the south.
Also, it is bordered by Khalifa Cemetery from the east, and Nile Corniche, Roda Island, and Manial Al-Roda from the west. This location puts Old Cairo Egypt, to the south of Downtown Cairo, and to the west of Cairo Citadel.
Old Cairo Egypt, has a central location that is, in fact, easily accessible from all over Egypt. But
where is Old Cairo?
It is exactly:
16 minutes away from Maadi
18 minutes away from
Mokattam
19 minutes away from Downtown Cairo

New Cairo City

Old Cairo Streets
Old Cairo, Egypt, is known for its historical streets, each of which has a story, and most of which keep their original old names.
The following list is an example of the well-known streets in Old Cairo Egypt:
Khan El-Khalili Street
It is one of the very well-known tourist attraction streets in Old Cairo, Egypt. The street is parallel to another well-known street, El-Mo’ez Ledin Allah Al-Fatimi Street.
It is named after its Fatimid founder, Emir Djaharks Al-Khalili from El-Khalil city in Palestine. Khan El-Khalili is famous for its monuments, souvenir bazars, and historical buildings and gates.
Al-Muizz Street
Al Muizz Street is also among the very popular streets in Old Cairo, Egypt. It is named after al-Muizz li-Din Allah, the Fatimid Caliph and the founder of the Fatimid Dynasty in Egypt. The street is listed on the UNESCO World Heritage List for its historical value.

Old Cairo History & Facts
Old Cairo, Egypt, is known for its historical value, which it has gained over different historical eras. The history of the area of Old Cairo, Egypt, started in the Pharaonic era, which was an important area on the Nile called “Memphis”.
It continued to be an important area during the Ptolemaic era, till the 4th century, when the Romans came to Egypt. When the Romans conquered Egypt, they built the well-known “Babylon Fortress,” whose remains are still present in today’s Old Cairo City.
The area stayed under Roman control until the 7th century, when Arabs entered Egypt and started to create districts in the area.
Their creations started with developing “Al Fustat”, one of the oldest and main districts in nowadays’ Old Cairo, and which currently hosts one of the most well-known mosques, Amr Ibn Al-As.
Later, during the Ayyubid state, another neighboring district was created, which is “Al Askar”. Even later, during the Mamluk state, Al Qataa’ (where the Ahmed Ibn Tulun mosque is found) was developed.
Those three districts (Fustat, Askar, and Qataa) are the main districts that form today’s Old Cairo, Egypt.
Over time, the historical weight of the city started to decline, and a new capital was chosen for Egypt during the Fatimid Dynasty, which is today’s Cairo.

The high investment potential (thanks to being a tourist district) your home holds, in case you wanted to rent it.

LOCATION: CENTRAL-CAIRO

About Central Cairo
Cairo Governorate​ is the vital core of Egypt. The city has many neighborhoods; however, it is Central Cairo is used to refer to Downtown (West El Balad), Heliopolis, and Old Cairo combined.
The name Cairo is the English word for Al-Qāhira (Al Kahera), translated as the conqueror or the victorious. Its name is used to reflect its historical resilience in combating all the invaders the city faced throughout history.
Also, its name was chosen to reflect the dominance and victory of the Fatimid dynasty, which originally created the city and gave it its name in 969 AD.
The
Cairo Central
we know today is the geographical connection between various capitals of older Islamic entities in Egypt. They include: El Fustat, Qata’i, Asker, the Fatimid Cairo, and the Khedivial Cairo. The city evolved over time to be today’s Central Cairo.
It holds significant historical, geographical, and cultural importance. Also, Cairo Governorate spans an extensive land area of
3,085 km²
.
Moreover, sometimes, Central Cairo is included in a bigger semi-official entity referred to as “Greater Cairo”. Greater Cairo also includes Giza Governorate and some of its suburbs, and Shubra El-Kheima.
Cairo Egypt Location​
Cairo Governorate is located in northeastern Egypt (Lower Egypt Region), near the Nile Delta, on the eastern bank of the Nile River.
Also, the city is bordered by Qalyubia Governorate from the north, and is bordered by Helwan from the south. Not to mention, Cairo Governorate is also bordered by Giza Governorate from the west, and is bordered by the Eastern Desert from the east.
This central location makes Cairo approximately:
30 minutes away from Cairo International Airport
30 minutes away from Maadi
40 minutes away from
New Cairo City
40 minutes away from
El Sheikh Zayed City
50 minutes away from 6 October City
50 minutes away from El Shorouk City
60 minutes away from
New Administrative Capital City
60 minutes away from
Mostakbal City
90 minutes away from Ain Sokhna
150 minutes away from
North Coast (Sahel)

Alexandria
is approximately 188 km, which takes around 2 and a half hours.

About El Lotus
El Lotus District is one of the top areas in New Cairo, located in the elevated region of Fifth Settlement. It is recognized as one of the most prestigious and significant residential areas.
Named for its unique architectural design and layout that resembles the shape of a lotus flower,
Ellotus
is bordered by North 90th Street to the north and South 90th Street to the south, with both streets interconnected by Club Street.
The district comprises 3 distinct neighborhoods: South Lotus, North Lotus, and New Lotus. Each neighborhood features endless facilities, luxurious residential units, and a premium location near major roads, making it an ideal and desirable place to live.
It is also worth noting that the zip code of El Lotus Fifth Settlement is 11835. El Lotus New Cairo is truly one of the perfect destinations for living. With its stunning architectural design, lush surroundings, and well-planned neighborhoods, it offers an exceptional lifestyle.
Residents enjoy a blend of modern amenities and a serene environment, making it an ideal choice for families and individuals alike.
El Lotus New Cairo Location
El Lotus is ideally positioned in the heart of
New Cairo
, nestled between the prominent South 90 and North 90 Streets, which are recognized as some of the most important roads in Tagamo3.
This advantageous location provides residents with convenient access to a variety of destinations, making daily commutes and travel effortless.
Situated just 9 km from
El Rehab City
via El Nasr Road, El Lotus New Cairo is a practical choice for those who work or spend time in that area.
Additionally,
New Cairo El Lotus
is located 20 km from Madinaty, offering residents proximity to another vibrant area in Cairo.
The area is also 16 km from the 2nd Ring Road, enhancing its accessibility to various parts of the city.
Moreover, El Lotus Egypt is only 24 km away from Nasr City via the Al Sadat Axis, and it provides direct access to Cairo’s Downtown, which is just 34.3 km away.
El Lotus New Cairo is a mere 23.3 km from Cairo International Airport, further solidifying its status as a central and highly accessible residential community.
Finally, Al Lotus is only 16 km away from
Cairo Festival City Mall
Being close to major roads allows residents to easily reach shopping centers, recreational facilities, and cultural landmarks, enhancing their overall living experience.
This prime location not only facilitates convenient commuting but also ensures that residents can enjoy the vibrant lifestyle that New Cairo has to offer, all while residing in a tranquil and well-planned community.

About South Investors
South Investors is one of the most elite residential and commercial neighborhoods in Fifth Settlement, New Cairo City. This neighborhood is known for its very close proximity to American University in Cairo’s (AUC) New Cairo Campus.
The neighborhood was named South Investors Area as it is in the southern area of 5th Settlement. Also, it is called the investors' area because it was intended from its development to host many investment and real estate projects.
This district has a prominent location that is easily accessible via all the main roads, such as 90th Street. Also, it is home to many upscale residential gated communities that number over 10.
The neighborhood also offers a fully-fledged living experience thanks to its comprehensive set of educational, recreational, and commercial facilities.  Also, since the area is an integral part of 5th Settlement, it has the same postal code as the area, which is 11835.

LOCATION: MAADI

About Maadi
Well known for its outstanding living experiences, Maadi is one of the most distinguished suburbs in Cairo, Egypt. During the 19th Century, it used to be the home for Europeans who came to work for Egyptian companies or the government.
Then, it became a unique residential destination for those seeking a tranquil lifestyle, characterized by fresh air, surrounded by elite amenities, and close to many destinations in Cairo.
El Maady is situated in the south of Cairo. It features a wide range of natural elements, restaurants, cafes, schools, and many other essential facilities. Moreover, this strategic location makes it one of the areas in which people most desire to live.
Recognized as one of the areas where both expats and locals enjoy their lives, El Maady is a top destination for families who are seeking a mix of fun, excitement, luxury, and convenience all in one place.
It flourished with artists, musicians, and foreign businessmen picking it as their home in Egypt, as it is one of the most bewitching suburban areas in Cairo.
Maadi Location in Cairo, Egypt
El Maady’s location may be geographically secluded, but definitely convenient; that’s why it is one of the best residential destinations in Cairo.
It is located in the south of Cairo, in a central spot that can be easily reached from and to. Moreover, the area is on the east bank of the Nile, and it is 12 km away from Downtown Cairo.
You can easily commute to and from El Maady because its prime location is approximately:
30 km away from New Cairo via the Ring Road, El-Moshir Tantawy Axis, or Gamal Abdel Nasser.

LOCATION: PORT-SAID
==================================================

About Port Said
Port Said City is one of the well-known 3 Canal Cities, which are Suez, Port Said, and Ismailia. It is a coastal city by the Mediterranean Sea, and it overlooks the Suez Canal. To be precise, the city is located at the northern entrance of the canal.
Also, the Suez Canal runs through the city, separating the entire neighborhoods of the govronormete from the district town and the last neighborhood in the city, which is Port Fouad.
The city spans an extensive land area of 1,344,961 square kilometers. The city is home to many well-known neighborhoods and districts, as well as many historical sites.
Moreover, the city has a major historical importance thanks to the role it took in the war in the 60’s and 70’s. This is why Port Said has many important national events, the most well-known of which is Victory Day, which is annually celebrated on the 23rd of December.
The name of the city was derived from the fact that the city is a coastal harbour on the canal and thus it's a port. In addition to that, its development started in the era of Khedive Mohamed Sa’id Pasha, ruler of Egypt, so the new city was called after his name.
Port Said Location​
Port Said City has a unique location in northeastern Egypt, on the Mediterranean Sea, at the northern entrance of the Suez Canal. It is the entrance point for the ships entering the Suez Canal from the Mediterranean Sea.
Also, Port Said Egypt City is bordered by the Mediterranean Sea to the north and by Ismailia Governorate to the south. Moreover, Port Said City is bordered by Manzala Lake, Damietta, Dakahlia, and Sharqia from the west.
It is also bordered by Port Fouad across the Suez Canal from the east. This location makes Port Said City:
1.5-hour drive (85 km) from Ismailia
2-hour drive (170 km) from Suez
3-hour drive (200 km) from
Cairo
3-hour drive (225 km) from
Ain Sokhna
4-hour drive (280 km) from
Alexandria
5-hour drive (440 km) from
North Coast- Sahel
Port Said Main Roads

Ahmed Hamdi Tunnel & Port Said Tunnel

Port Said City is divided into seven main districts in addition to Port Fouad District, totaling eight main neighborhoods. Each of which has its own facilities and services. Those neighborhoods are as follows:
Port Fouad District Town (separated from the city by the Suez Canal, reached by boat)

Port Said City​ History​
Port Said City has always had a significant historical value rooted in its strategic location as one of the Canal Cities.
The city’s development started back in 1859 when the French Diplomat Ferdinand de Lesseps suggested digging the Suez Canal. As a result of the suggestion, Khedive Mohamed Sa’id Pasha declared the beginning of Port Said’s development to be a residential city as well as an industrial port for Egypt.
Later in the 60’s and 70’s, and due to its strategic location on the Suez Canal, the city played a crucial role in the war.

About New Capital Gardens
New Capital Gardens is a fourth-generation city, ideally located in New Administrative Capital. It was developed and brilliantly planned east of Badr City.
The city boasts a wide range of housing options, built to offer 2.6 million people a blend of sustainability, luxury, and comfort. 33 thousand acres of New Capital City's total land area (170,000 acres) was dedicated to the development of Hadayek Al Asema.
It boasts a myriad of impeccable services and facilities, aimed at its residents’ seamless, hassle-free lifestyle. The development of New Capital City was announced in 2015. It aligns with Egypt’s 2030 vision, and it perfectly blends:
Commercial and administrative projects
Sustainability measures
Smart solutions
Luxurious gated communities in its various residential districts

LOCATION: RAS-EL-HEKMA
==================================================

About Ras El Hekma
Ras El Hekma is one of the most attractive North Coast areas that has been attracting both; Egyptian vacationers as well as tourists lately.
The area is very well-known for its pristine beaches, white sands, lavish resorts, and perfect climate.
Despite being a coastal area that has always been there, the importance of Ras El Hekma has been very prominent since February 2024 after an important investment deal signed by the Egyptian Government.
Ras El Hikma is considered a perfect gateway for both; Egyptian vacationers and summer homeowners on the one hand, and tourists on the other hand.
History & Details of Ras El Hekma
The first time the Ras El Hekma area hosted a summer destination was in the early 1940s when King Farouk of Egypt decided to have his summer home in a magnificent coastal area in Marsa Matrouh Governorate.
The area became very well-known after the Egyptian Government and the Government of Abu Dhabithe signed a $35 billion deal to develop this area. This development project was beneficial for the Egyptian side in many dimensions. Firstly, it has pumped currency into the Egyptian economy (in the foreign direct investment (FDI) sector) which helped the country overcome its economic crisis (then).
Ras El Hekma is considered the eastern part of Marsa Matrouh governorate and it rolls over 40,600 acres of land in addition to enjoying a width of 4km into the coastal strip.
Ras El Hekma Location
Ras El Hikma is located on the top point of the
North Coast
. The area stretches from km 178 to km 220 on the International Coastal Road which is also known as the Alexandria-Marsa Matrouh Road.
This location makes Ras El Hikma:
85 km (almost 60 minutes) away from Marsa Matrouh
50 km (almost 45 minutes) away from
Al Dabaa
240 km (almost 150 minutes) away from
Alexandria
Don’t forget to check out
Nawy’s Sahel Map
to know the exact locations of any of the Sahel Compounds and calculate the distance between them.
From Cairo To Ras El Hikma
Bearing the strategic location of Ras El Hekma in mind, Cairo is 140 km away from Ras El Hikma, the drive that could be taken in almost 2 hours -120 minutes.
Remember that the main highways in the area are Fouka Road, El Dabaa Road, and the International Coastal Road.
Ras El Hekma Compounds
Ras El Hekma is home to many high-end resorts that offer the perfect summer gateway. These upscale compounds and resorts include:
Solare by Misr Italia Properties
Solaré Resort is one of the upscale summer gateways on the North Coast. The resort rolls over 386 acres of land with a beachfront of 1 km and an elevation of 31 meters above sea level.
The resort features a wide set of high-end amenities including 60,000 square meters of lagoons,15,000 square meters of waterbodies,2 international boutique hotels, a retail area, a sports area, clubhouses, and 18 swimming pools.
Lastly, Solare enjoys a premium location on the 199th kilo on the International Coastal Road.
Hacienda West by Palm Hills Developments
Hacienda West is one of the awesome creations on the North Coast. The resort is an all-inclusive summer gateway for vacationers and residents.
Hacienda West North Coast features many upscale amenities such as a branded hotel, community hub, fully integrated sports area, gym, restaurants, kids area, private lagoons, and a beach lounge.
Last but not least, the resort falls on the kilo 208th on the International Coastal Road.
Salt by Tatweer Misr
Salt is a unique summer destination rolling over 294.5 acres of land with an 830-meter beachfront.
The resort features many high-end amenities that include pools, lagoons, pocket parks, outdoor spaces, and lush greens.
Finally, Salt is located on the 185th km of the International Coastal Road.
June by SODIC
June is a 280-acre summer resort that is considered one of the finest summer destinations. The project features a wide array of upscale amenities including a clubhouse, sports club, swimming pools, yoga area, wellness center, a shopping center, and verdant landscaping.
The resort falls on the kilo 193 on the International Coastal Road.
Gaia by Al Ahly Sabbour Developments
Gaia is an opulent summer destination designed by the award-winning designer Chapman Taylar. The resort rolls over 280 acres of land with 65% of this area taken to landscaping and greenery.
The amenities offered in the project include 45000 square meters of water bodies, swimming pools, swimmable lagoons, a hotel, a kid's area, a football court, a commercial strip, fine dining restaurants, pools, and a gym.
Finally, you will find Gaia on the kilo 193 on the International Coastal Road.
Koun by Mabany Edris
Koun is one of the unique summer destinations that spans 106 acres,85% of which is dedicated to lush greens and landscaping.
The amenities exhibited in the project include a 34,000 sqm beachfront, swimming pools for all ages, and 10 acres of lagoons.
The resort lies on the 201st km on the International Coastal Road.
Hyde Park North - Seashore by Hyde Park
Seashore is a perfectly designed summer resort rolling over 240 acres of land and master planned by EDSA and SB.
The resort features many upscale amenities such as a 550-meter beach clubhouse, restaurants, 25 beach entries, swimming pools, serviced apartments, fiber optics services, a promenade, a green spine, water sports, a security gated entrance, staff housing, a commercial strip, and a 5-star hotel.
The resort is placed on the 214th km on the International Coastal Road.
Cali Coast Ras El Hekma by MAVEN DEVELOPMENTS
Cali Coast is a 245-acre resort featuring a 600-meter beachfront, elevation of 8 levels, and a 30-acre beach area.
The resort boasts a wide range of upscale amenities that include 150,000 square meters of water bodies, 4.5,000 km of beach line, 87% greenery, landscaping, and water bodies.
Lastly, the resort is located on kilo 193 of the International Coastal Road.
Safia - Ras El Hekma by IL Cazar Developments
Safia is one of the upscale summer resorts created to be a beach heaven. The resort features many high-end facilities such as verdant landscaping, lush greens, various water bodies, a commercial area, swimming pools, and a beach area.
Safia Resort is located on the 186th km of the International Coastal Road.
Direction White by Arabella
Direction White is a 290-acre resort on the North Coast that was created to be a summer paradise.
The resort features many high-end amenities including vast greenery, natural landscapes, pedestrian, jogging, and cycling trails, a wide beachfront, and many swimming pools.
Direction White Resort is located on the kilo 192 of the International Coastal Road.
Mountain View Ras El Hekma by Mountain View
Mountain View Ras El Hekma is one of the marvelous creations on the North Coast of Egypt. The resort is created upon Greek-style architecture over a land area of 121 acres.
Evia features many high-end amenities including water sports, beaches, swimmable lagoons, and swimming pools.
Finally, you will find Evia on the 200th km of the International Coastal Road.
Gaia Cabanas by Melee Development

About Ras Sudr
Ras Sudr is an Egyptian city located on the Gulf of Suez along the Red Sea. It is part of the South Sinai Governorate, and it has a rich history, dating back to Ancient Egypt, the times of Prophet Moses, Christ, the Greeks, and the Romans.
Over time, it has become an increasingly popular tourist destination due to its tranquil sandy shores, minimal seaweed, low salt levels, and calm waters. Ras Sudr is located approximately 200 kilometers from Cairo, accessible via the Martyr Ahmed Hamdi Tunnel.
Ras Sudr Egypt Location
Ras Sudr Governorate
is a city located on the Gulf of Suez, along the eastern coast of Egypt. It falls within the South Sinai Governorate, one of the governorates that make up the Sinai Peninsula.
The city is approximately 200 kilometers from Cairo, easily accessible via the Martyr Ahmed Hamdi Tunnel.
This strategic location on the Red Sea coast has contributed to Ras Sudr's historical significance and its current status as a popular tourist destination.
The city's proximity to the Red Sea and the Gulf of Suez provides easy access to the region's beautiful beaches, calm waters, and diverse marine life. Ras Sudr is approximately:
1 hour and 20 minutes away from Suez.
2 hours from
Ain Sokhna
.

Distance from Cairo to Ras Sudr
The distance from Cairo to Ras Sudr is approximately 199.3 kilometers. It typically takes around 2 hours and 38 minutes when traveling via Route 50M and the El Qantra Shark - Ras Sedr Road (also known as Ras Sedr - Al Shahid Ahmed Hamdy Tunnel).
This convenient route makes Ras Sudr easily accessible for those looking to enjoy its serene beaches and attractions, providing a quick getaway from the bustling city of Cairo.
Key Roads in Ras Sudr
Thanks to its prime location on the Gulf of Suez, Ras Sudr, Egypt, is easily reachable via several key roads and axes, such as:

Ras Sudr Map
Ras Sudr is a part of the South Sinai Governorate. With a history that spans back to the Ancient Egyptians, the city has evolved into a popular tourist destination. Visitors are drawn to its peaceful sandy beaches, which feature minimal seaweed, low salt content, and calm waters.
The Ras Sudr map encompasses many of the city’s popular attractions, which include, but are not limited to:
El-Gendy Fortress (or Sudr Fortress): This historic stone fortress was constructed during Salah al-Din's campaigns against the Crusaders.
Pharaoh's Baths (Hammamat Faraoun): Renowned hot springs that emerge from the mountains, these baths are a significant tourist attraction.
El-Maghara Engravings: Ancient inscriptions that highlight the region's historical importance.
Ras Sudr Sulfur Springs: Known for their healing properties, these springs are a draw for wellness tourists.
The city is divided into three main areas, which are Wadi Sudr, Sudr, and Abu Suwayrah. The population is primarily made up of Sinai Bedouins, who reside in areas such as Wadi Sudr and Abu Suwayrah, while Sudr serves as the city center.
Ras Sudr features several tourist villages and hotels along its beaches, attracting an increasing number of both Egyptian and international tourists.

Activities & Things to Do in Ras Sedr
Ras Sudr Egypt, offers a mix of historical, cultural, and natural attractions. The top things to do and places to visit in the city include:
Al Jundi Castle
A historical landmark, Al Jundi Castle is a fascinating site that reflects the architectural and cultural heritage of the area. It provides a great opportunity to explore the past of Ras Sudr.
The Pharaoh’s Baths (Hammam Pharaon)
These natural hot springs are believed to have therapeutic properties. The baths are located in a cave and are a popular spot for relaxation and wellness seekers.
Ain Ras Sidr
A natural spring in the area, Ain Ras Sidr, is a serene spot for visitors to enjoy the beauty of nature. It is perfect for those looking to unwind and connect with the environment.
Moses Springs (Oyoun Mousa)
Located near Ras Sidr, Moses Springs is a significant religious and historical site. According to tradition, these springs are where Prophet Moses struck a rock to bring forth water for his people.
Kitesurfing and Water Sports
Ras Sudr is famous for its kitesurfing centers, such as Soul Kitesurfing and 360 Kitesurfing Centre. Visitors can also enjoy other water sports like paddleboarding, kayaking, and windsurfing.
Relaxing on the Beach
The beaches of Ras Sudr are perfect for relaxation, sunbathing, and enjoying the stunning views of the Red Sea. Many resorts offer private beach access and facilities for a comfortable experience.
Kitesurfing Centers in Ras Sudr​
Ras Sudr is renowned as one of the best kitesurfing destinations in Egypt, thanks to its ideal wind conditions, shallow lagoons, and proximity to Cairo.
The area is home to numerous kitesurfing centers that cater to both beginners and experienced kitesurfers. Some of the top facilities in the area include, but are not limited to:
Soul Kitesurfing Center

About New Sphinx
New Sphinx City is one of the new, smart, fourth-generation cities developed by the New Urban Communities Authority for Planning and Projects. It was developed as part of the government’s plan to build 14 new cities to attract residents and ease the residential load on Cairo and the Delta.
The city is located near Western Cairo, approved by Ministerial Decree 910 on November 1, 2020. Covering an approximate area of 76,931 acres, the City​ is filled to the brim with endless facilities, making it an ideal place to live.
New Sphinx is equipped with a range of services, including residential areas, educational institutions, healthcare facilities, and commercial spaces. All were designed to enhance residents' quality of life.
Also, strategically located to enhance connectivity with Cairo and the surrounding areas, the city features well-planned roads for convenient commuting.
Additionally, the City emphasizes green spaces and recreational areas, promoting a healthy lifestyle and community engagement.
With its modern infrastructure and comprehensive range of services, the city is positioned as a perfect area to live, attracting families and individuals seeking comfort away from the hustle and bustle of central Cairo.
New Sphinx City Location in Egypt
New Sphinx City is located between Cairo, Monufia, and Giza, near 6 October City and Sheikh Zayed, on the Cairo - Alexandria Desert Road. The city is just a few minutes away from many key attractions and cities.

About Sahl Hasheesh
Sahl Hasheesh Red Sea Egypt​ is a privately developed and owned coastal resort city by Egyptian Resorts Company (ERC), and it is situated in Hurghada Governorate.
This city is considered the flagship project by the company on the Red Sea’s coastline, and it is only 20 kilometers south of Hurghada Airport. It is not a mere tourist destination or only a summer gateway.
Rather, it is a fully-fledged all-year-round residential community bustling with high-end real estate developments, top-tier facilities, and top-notch services.
Also, Sahl Hasheesh is one of the perfect investment spots in the Red Sea Egypt. Thanks to its pristine beaches, upscale amenities, and first-rate accommodations, it acts as both a tourist attraction spot and a home for many first- and second-home owners who want to live or invest.
In fact, Sahl Hasheesh is a self-sufficient city with a 10,000+ m3 per day desalination plant, extensive water storage, supply and irrigation networks, 41+ kilometers of internal roadways, self-sustained power, and telecommunications networks.
Sahl Hasheesh Location
Sahl Hasheesh Egypt, enjoys a premium location on the Red Sea coastline. It is situated between Safaga and Hurghada on the Hurghada - Ismaila Road.
This location makes the city very close to
Hurghada City
and thus gives Sahl Hasheesh easy access to its livable facilities. In fact, it is a mere 25 km away.
Distance from Hurghada to Sahl Hasheesh​
Sahl Hasheesh Egypt enjoys a central location that is within proximity to Hurghada City. It is around 25 km south of Hurghada (a 15-minute drive). Also, it is 20 km away from Hurghada International Airport, which is almost a 10-minute drive.
This location makes
Sahl Hasheesh Hurghada Egypt
44 minutes (55.8 km) away from
El Gouna
. Finally, it is important to note that the area is 28 minutes away from the well-known Makadi Bay, close to Hurghada.
Distance from Cairo to Sahl Hasheesh​ Egypt
Concerning the distance between Cairo and Sahl Hasheesh, it is 490 km, taking a 5-hour car ride or a 1-hour flight.

74800062.8 square meter

Later, the Egyptian Resorts Company (the master developer of the city) started to build and invest in more zones in the city. Moreover, the city’s development has two main phases: Phase I and Phase II.
Those phases host more than 6 residential compounds with more than 1,500 residential units delivered and more than 6 world-renowned hotels with 3,000 hotel rooms in operation.

Old Town Sahl Hasheesh Egypt
Old Town Sahl Hasheesh is the oldest part of the city. It is characterized by its unique old-style architecture that brings the vibes of old golden summer days along with the modern facilities of the city.
In the Old Town of Sahl Hasheesh, you will find the Plaza, which is filled to the brim with outdoor spaces, event spaces, and gathering spaces, and it is considered one of the most visited places in the area.
Also, the Old Town features “Old Town Corniche” also known as "Old Town Road", and it exhibits walking lanes, shopping stores, F&B outlets, and many public sittings.

About Sidi Heneish
Sidi Heneish Bay is among the numerous magnificent North Coast- Sahel areas. The bay got its name Sidi Heneish, “Sidi” meaning master or lord ,and “Heneish” which means baby snake.
Despite being a relatively small-sized area compared to other Sahel areas, Sidi Heneish enjoys beautiful beaches, sugar-like sands, and many top-tier resorts, all of which offer the best summer experience possible.
Sidi Heneish Location
Sidi Heneish enjoys a premium location in
North Coast
stretching from the kilo 221 to the kilo 250 on the International Coastal Road also known as Alexandria-Marsa Matrouh Road.
This location makes Sidi Heneish:
4 hours (392.8 km) from Cairo
2 hours 45 minutes (245.4 km) from Alexandria
1 hour 30 minutes (149.1 km) from
Al Alamein
1 hour 14 minutes (111.1 km) from

LOCATION: 6TH-OF-OCTOBER-CITY
==================================================

About 6th of October City
6th of October is one of the satellite cities developed to be a major residential, commercial, and industrial zone in West Cairo. The city is known to be one of the most tranquil and hassle-free cities on the west bank of the Nile.
Also, 6 October City is most known for its Smart Village, which serves as a center for the IT industry in Egypt. It has many upscale local and international companies operating there. The city is located in northern Egypt, creating one of the largest neighborhoods in Giza Governorate.
The city, whose development started in 1979 according to the presidential decree number 504, was named after the National Army Day. It has a growing population and is expected to host more than 6,000,000,000 people by 2027.
Thanks to the smart initiatives of the Egyptian government and well-known real estate developers, the city now has many upscale compounds, a premium network of roads, and many educational, commercial, administrative, healthcare, and recreational facilities.
6 October Location
6th of October City enjoys a strategic prime location that is beneficial in two directions. On the one hand, it is close to the major city attractions, and on the other hand, it is still away from the crowd of Cairo.
The city is situated on the West Bank of the River Nile to the west of Cairo in Giza Governorate, adjacent to Sheikh Zayed City. It is directly on Wahat Road.
This location enables October City to enjoy easy access to and from major destinations, airports, and high-end residential compounds, making it the ultimate option for those who want to enjoy a calm,traffic-free life and yet stay close to the city.
To be more specific, the exact location of 6th of October City is:
16 km away from Sheikh Zayed City
17 km away from the Great Pyramids of Giza
32 km away from Cairo’s downtown
64 km away from New Cairo
71 km away from New Administrative Capital
72 km away from Cairo International Airport
6 October Main Roads
6th of October City, Al Giza Desert, enjoys its connection to many main roads that either pass by or through the city or that are near the city, linking it to other parts of the town.
The main roads that are across 6th of October City include:
Cairo - Alexandria Desert Road
26th of July Corridor
El Wahat Road

Middle Ring Road
Dabaa Axis

Remember that a monorail line is anticipated to soon connect the Giza governorate with 6 October City, Sheikh Zayed, and the upcoming extensions of 6 October City. It will begin at the Gameat El Dewal station of Cairo Metro Line 3.
6 October City Land Area & Map
6 October City spans an extensive land area of 119,200 acres. This land area was well-planned, offering a map that reveals various neighborhoods and facilities.
This design offers the city’s residents a comprehensive, fully-fledged living experience. The 6th of October map has the following:
More than 10 residential neighborhoods

It was constructed in accordance with the new 6th of October City division to serve as an extension of the city and house the greatest number of people in new housing and service projects.

6 October Weather​
The weather of 6 October is characterized by dry and arid desert conditions. These conditions make 6th of October City enjoy a hot desert (BWh) environment. Because of its close vicinity to Cairo and Giza, it has a climate that is extremely similar to theirs.
That being said, for a variety of reasons, some locations on October 6th are a little windier and colder at night than central Cairo and Giza. Compared to the heavily crowded centers of Cairo and Giza, this is mostly because buildings and infrastructure are typically more widely separated and have more open areas, which makes it easier for the wind to blow through.
Furthermore, compared to the moist, humid region near the Nile, the desert where the city was constructed is typically colder and drier.

About Mostakbal City
Mostakbal City in New Cairo is owned and developed by El Mostakbal for Urban Development, along with its extension, Midar Development Company. The city was created to offer more space and energy for the growing population with wider investment and housing opportunities.
The Mostakbal City, East Cairo's first smart green city, represents a fresh take on contemporary life. It was created through in-depth market research to satisfy the demands and expectations of developers, residents, and investors.
It features wide green spaces and full utilities, all carefully designed to guarantee sustainable development for the present and the future. Mostakbal City, which covers 11,000 acres, is home to 42+ projects and 28+ developers.
The city is created with the utmost means of luxury and comfort thanks to its bustling facilities and nearby amenities. Also, it has a prime location that is easily accessible via many roads.
Moreover, Mostakbal City​​ is home to many upscale, unique residential gated communities offering an elevated living experience.
Mostakbal City Location
Mostakbal City was carefully built with maximum accessibility in mind and it is well situated along Cairo Suez Road between kilometers 46 and 51 East Cairo on the Cairo Suez Road.
Mostakbal City is situated at a prime location in the center of New Cairo, surrounded by vibrant cities like
Madinaty
, El Shorouk, Rehab City, and New Capital.
New Capital is around 15 minutes away from Mostakbal City with direct access to the New Cairo Capital's rapid train station and international airport. It offers convenient access to Egypt's best educational institutions, including the American University in Cairo and the vibrant events of Road 90.
Additionally, the city is just:
45 minutes from Al Ein El Sokhna
A 20-minute drive from Cairo International Airport
10 minutes away from 5th Settlement

Mostakbal City Map & Master Plan
With five prosperous phases and a master plan for a fully connected metropolis, the historic project is designed to house over a million people and allocates half of its land area to roads and green open spaces.
With its expansive dimensions and wide range of lifestyle options, Mostakbal City Egypt lays the groundwork for sustainable modern living in the future.
Its smart city architecture and self-sufficient environment enable residents to experience full well-being on all fronts while connecting with nature and one another.
The stunning
5,200-acre or 22,394,419 square meters
Mostakbal City, the most integrated "Mega Green City" in New Cairo, is master-planned to feature self-sufficient dwelling alternatives, world-class recreational amenities, and bustling commercial zones.
Reputable developers and investors are drawn to phases three and four, which provide upscale residential zones spanning 1607 and 1875 acres, respectively. It places a strong emphasis on sustainable development to address the demands of the current and future environments.
Every phase will benefit from a variety of top-notch recreational amenities, continuous entertainment, and a world of experiences not available elsewhere, all connected by a thriving commercial spine that runs the length of the project.
Mostakbal City Phases
Phase one, which covers 1490 acres, serves as a hub for upscale housing close to prestigious educational establishments.
It serves as its essential core and offers a medium-sized housing complex that is independent and conveniently located near prestigious universities like Cairo's American University.
Along the Suez Road, the second phase serves as a regional service center spanning more than 2046 acres, providing residents and investors with direct access to the commercial, administrative, medical, hotel, and recreational facilities necessary for their development.
Taking advantage of the city's growth, the third and fourth phases are upscale residential neighborhoods that draw in more investors and residents looking for exceptional value.
The fifth phase, which occupies 3755 acres, is a multipurpose administrative, commercial, and residential center that has a prime location close to the new Administrative Capital's economic core.
Mostakbal City Smart Design
With its own operating and management system, the developer of the city makes sure that all solid waste management, irrigation, and landscaping services are always provided for the convenience of the people.
Through the use of cutting-edge intelligent technology, the city offers intelligent communication.
E-payments, convenient parking, and public transit that is on par with international megacities worldwide, all of which are accessible to residents via a smartphone application.
With its own utilities and network management system, Mostakbal City provides independent gas and potable water pipelines. It also offers a self-sufficient electricity power plant for equitable distribution.
Also, a private security service covering all city roads and gates to meet the highest sustainability and safety standards for a hassle-free living environment.
Mostakbal City is equipped with optical fiber communication networks to provide the best connection possible throughout the day and is poised to develop into a thriving business center, a hub for residential investment, and a destination for leisure.
The city's distinctive urban design was skillfully developed using in-depth market research to offer workable solutions that surpass homeowners' expectations and draw in Egypt's top real estate developers.
