The city of Mostakbal was skillfully designed to revitalize its inhabitants. The entire city was designed to encircle families with green, open areas in recognition of the therapeutic power of nature. This would lower stress levels, improve health, and encourage social contact in a lush setting.
Economic prosperity, well-being, and societal advantages are conceptually linked by people. Thus, every element of Mostakbal City contributes to a balanced way of living that emphasizes cutting emissions and waste, increasing open spaces, and promoting recycling.

LOCATION: MOKATTAM

About Mokattam
El Mokattam, Egypt, is one of the magical districts in Greater Cairo. This area overlooks a unique view thanks to being located over a wide plateau; this is why it is sometimes referred to as El Mokattam Hills or El Mokattam Mountain.
Living in Mokattam allows residents to enjoy the magnificent sunrise view from the mountain top or exquisite walks by the mesmerizing El Mokattam Corniche.
It is a part of Cairo Governorate in the Eastern Desert plateau area. It is situated in the southern area of the city, adjacent to Old Cairo and El Fustat, and it is under the supervision of the Mokattam District Presidency.
El Mokattam Location
Mokattam, Egypt, has a prime location in Cairo Governorate. It is close to other residential areas, such as Nasr City and
El Maadi
.
The ideal location of El Mokattam is around:
23 minutes from
New Cairo City
25 minutes away from Cairo International Airport
26 minutes away from Downtown Cairo
27 minutes away from Heliopolis
32 minutes away from Al Maadi
45 minutes away from
New Capital City
48 minutes away from Mostakbal City
50 minutes away from
6 October City
57 minutes away from El Sheikh Zayed City
Key Roads in Mokattam
El Mokattam is easily accessible through several major roads and axes. It is in proximity to:
Salah Salem Road
Ring Road
El-Moshir Tantawy Axis
Cairo - Suez Road
El Mokattam Egypt Map
The Mokattam Egypt map shows that the area is composed mainly of 3 plateaus: the highest one, the middle one (El Hadaba El Wosta Mokattam​), and the lower one.
The district is formed as a medium-height triangular district with an area of ​​14 square kilometers. It extends in the form of a limestone ledge, starting from the bottom at a height of 60 meters towards the east, and its maximum height is 140 meters.
It is convex in the area towards the castle, and its height is 240 meters. El Drassa and Manshit Nasser extend from it in areas with steep slopes resulting from the quarrying activity that contributed to the disruption of its layers.
El Mokattam, Egypt, has many well-known districts, including Nafoura Square, Diplomatic District, Corniche zone, and Mokattam Street.
Lastly, it is bordered by El Bassatin District and Maadi District from the south, and by El Khalifa District and El Sayyda District from the West. Also, it is adjacent to Al Abassaia from the north and Nasr City and New Cairo from the east.

About Makadi
Makadi Bay is one of the exceptional beach towns by the Red Sea Riviera (a coastline by the Red Sea that includes magnificent cities such as Ras Sudr, Sharm el Sheikh, Dahab, Nuweiba, and Taba). It is an integral part of Hurghada City, Egypt.
Makadi Bay, Egypt, is known for its refreshing weather all year round, its picturesque coral reefs, the crystal clear waters, sandy beaches, and various water activities one can practice there.
It is a premium summer destination with many beautiful beaches, exclusive resorts and hotels, and top-tier facilities and services.
Makadi Bay Location In Egypt
Makadi Bay, Egypt, enjoys a premium location on the Red Sea Riviera, between the Eastern Desert and the Red Sea, in Hurghada City, Red Sea Governorate. This premium location puts the bay 30 km south of Hurghada.
Also, this location puts Makadi:
26.7 km (31 minutes) away from
Soma Bay
30.6 km (35 minutes) away from Hurghada International Airport
46 km (44 minutes) away from
Hurghada City
62.7 km (52 minutes) away from El Gouna
370 km (4 hours) away from
Ain Sokhna
491 km (5 hours) away from Cairo International Airport
494 km (5 hours) away from Cairo (1-hour flight)
709 km (7 hours 20 minutes) away from
Alexandria
Makadi Bay Major Roads
Makadi Bay is easily accessible from main roads, making it a convenient summer destination. These roads include:
Safaga Road
Ismailia - Hurghada Road
Cairo - Alexandria Desert Road
Suez Road
Distance From Hurghada To Makadi Bay​
Makadi Bay is privileged with its proximity to Hurghada, which makes it an easily accessible neighborhood and takes advantage of all the facilities found in Hurghada City. It is just 30 km south of Hurghada City.
Also, it is just 46 km away (around 44 minutes) from the city’s center. Lastly, as one of the major landmarks of the city, Makadi Bay, Egypt, is just 30.6 km (almost a 35-minute ride) away from Hurghada International Airport.
Makadi Bay Map

About New Heliopolis
New Heliopolis is a prominent urban development located east of Cairo Governorate Egypt, covering an extensive area of over 5,888 acres.
Established under Presidential Decree No. 193 of 1995. It is managed by the Heliopolis Company for Housing and Development and is considered the natural extension of Heliopolis.
The city features a strategic location, modern infrastructure, upscale residential and commercial projects, and family-friendly facilities, making it an ideal destination for families and investors.
It was designed to address the challenges of population density and promote sustainable urban development across the country. Simply, the city was established with the goal of alleviating pressure on existing urban areas while providing modern living solutions.
New Heliopolis Location in Cairo
New Heliopolis City is strategically situated and well-connected to major roads and neighboring areas. These are the key things you should know about its location in Cairo:
It is linked to the Cairo - Ismailia Road from the north and the Cairo - Suez Road from the south.
It borders Madinaty to the south, the original settlement of
El Shorouk
to the west, and the satellite city of Badr to the east. This connectivity is further enhanced by its access to the Regional Ring Road, which links it to all parts of Greater Cairo.
The city is conveniently located just 25 minutes away from the districts of Heliopolis and Nasr City, making it an attractive residential and commercial hub for those seeking proximity to Cairo's key areas while enjoying a quieter, more modern environment.

LOCATION: HELIOPOLIS

About Heliopolis
Heliopolis, Cairo, Egypt, is a prestigious city renowned for its rich history, well-planned architecture, high-standard hotels, and endless facilities.
Developed in the early 20th century, Heliopolis was designed as a modern suburb and has evolved into one of Cairo's most sought-after residential, commercial, and entertainment areas.
Heliopolis Cairo Egypt, which translates to "City of the Sun," has deep roots in ancient Egyptian history. The area was once home to the ancient sun temple and has been a significant site for many historical events.
Today, remnants of its glorious past can still be seen in various monuments and structures. The postal code for Heliopolis, Cairo, is 11757, which plays a vital role in ensuring efficient mail delivery within this vibrant district of Cairo.
Heliopolis Location In Cairo Governorate​
Heliopolis Area Egypt, has an ideal location near everything residents need, from the major roads to the transport stations, metro stations, schools, and new cities in Cairo. Situated just 10 km from downtown Cairo and approximately 5 km from Cairo International Airport, Heliopolis serves as a well-connected hub for both residents and visitors alike.
Heliopolis, Egypt, located in northeastern Cairo, is a historically rich district that blends ancient heritage with modern urban development. The area’s borders are as follows:
North: El-Nozha district and Cairo International Airport
South: Nasr City
East: Ring Road and
New Cairo
West: Downtown Cairo and the historic heart of the city
Heliopolis Major Roads
Heliopolis is strategically connected by several major roads that facilitate easy access to and from the district. These roads play a crucial role in the daily commute for residents and visitors alike.
The main roads passing by and through the area include:
Salah Salem Street

El Merghany and El Hegaz Streets

Autostrad & Ring Road (connecting to New Cairo and Giza)
Heliopolis Map & Districts
Heliopolis Cairo Egypt, is a vibrant urban area known for its rich history, unique architecture, and modern lifestyle.
The area encompasses both the ancient city of Heliopolis and the 20th-century suburb of Masr El Gedida, offering a unique glimpse into Egypt's evolution over millennia.
Masr El Gedida, originally established as a garden city in the early 20th century, is now a vibrant urban district. Key districts within Heliopolis Cairo Governorate​ include:
Almaza
Ard El Golf
Roxy
Korba
Muntazah
Sheraton
Bustan
These neighborhoods are known for their upscale residential buildings, historic landmarks, and vibrant commercial activities.
Korba
El Korba is a famous district in Heliopolis area renowned for its unique early 20th-century architecture and vibrant cultural scene.
Built by Belgian industrialist Baron Édouard Empain in the early 1900s, El Korba was designed as a cosmopolitan suburb that blended European and Islamic architectural styles.
El Korba has long been a cultural hub in Cairo. The area is home to several landmarks, including the Basilica of Notre Dame, commissioned by Baron Empain and modeled after the Hagia Sophia in Istanbul.
In recent years, El Korba has undergone revitalization efforts to preserve its architectural heritage while accommodating modern needs. These initiatives aim to maintain the district's unique character and ensure its continued role as a vibrant part of Cairo's urban landscape.
What is Korba Heliopolis famous for? It’s famous for its numerous cafes, restaurants, and shops that maintain the area's historical charm.
Sheraton
Sheraton is a well-established residential area located in the northeastern part of Heliopolis, Cairo. It is officially part of the El Nozha district and is administratively designated as Sheraton el-Matar.
The area is just a short drive away from the airport, making it convenient for travelers. Sheraton is well-connected to key roads such as Al Nasr Road and Salah Salem Street, facilitating smooth transportation across the city.

:
a pioneering educational institution, established in 1986 and inaugurated in its current form in 1996, it stands as the first children's museum in the Middle East and North Africa, located at 34 Abo Bakr El Seddik Street, Heliopolis, Cairo.

Baron Empain Palace
: also known as Le Palais Hindou (The Hindu Palace), is a striking historical mansion that was built in 1905 for Édouard Empain, a Belgian industrialist and transportation magnate. The palace is renowned for its unique architectural style that blends Indian influences with local design elements.

LOCATION: DOWNTOWN-CAIRO

About Downtown Cairo
Downtown Cairo (West El Balad) is the vibrant heart of the city. It blends culture, history, and various architectural masterpieces.
In addition to being a convenient place to live for those seeking connectivity to anywhere around Cairo, West El-Balad is filled with many popular destinations, important facilities, and recreational activities.
The Downtown Cairo location in Egypt offers its residents and visitors a seamless commute to and from the area. It is ideally situated between Midan Talaat Harb and Qasr El Nil.
Thanks to the several main roads passing through West El Balad, you can easily move to and from it, whether to the east of Cairo (such as New Cairo) or to the west of Cairo (such as 6 of October City).
Where is Downtown Cairo?
The location of Downtown Cairo is between Talaat Harb Street and Qasr El Nil. By the southern end of West El Balad lies Midan El Tahrir, one of the iconic destinations in Egypt.
Downtown Cairo boasts an ideal location in Egypt that can be easily accessed and commuted from. For instance:
It is approximately 3 km away from Garden City.
West El Balad is around 4 km away from El Zamalek, Dokki, and Mohandessin.
Downtown is around 15 km away from Maadi and El Mokattam.
Downtown Egypt around an 18-km drive from Downtown Cairo to Nasr City and Heliopolis.
Cairo International Airport is 20 km away from West El-Balad.
Downtown Cairo is approximately 22 km away from the Giza Pyramids.
Furthermore, one of the reasons behind
Down Town Egypt
boasting a strategic location in Egypt is that it is not a short drive away from both the east and west of Cairo, as it is approximately:
28 km away from
El Sheikh Zayed City
.
30 km away from
New Cairo
.
A 40-km drive to
6th of October City
.
70 km from
New Capital City
.

Downtown Cairo Map & Streets
The Downtown Cairo in Egypt map is divided into several districts and streets. Each exhibits its own charm, facilities, and activities. They reflect the

Downtown Cairo Postal Code
The facilities, buildings, and streets of Downtown Cairo in Egypt carry different postal codes; for instance:
Abdel Khalek Tharwat Street’s postal code is 11511.
The postal code of Tahrir Square in Downtown Cairo is 11512.
Bab El Louk postal code is 11513.
The Ministries Building postal code is 11514.
The Television Building on Nile Corniche postal code is 11515.

Best Downtown Cairo Real Estate Projects
There are various residential, commercial, and administrative real estate projects in Downtown Cairo. They boast top-tier amenities and luxurious units. They are ideally situated in Maspero Triangle, which extends over 77 acres.
These developments are Maspero Business Tower, Maspero Nile Hights, and Maspero Mall.
Maspero Nile Heights
Maspero Nile Heights
is one of the best real estate projects in Downtown Cairo. It is composed of 24 stories and boasts a high-end set of administrative offices. It was developed by City Edge Developments, which implemented a broad array of services and facilities in the project.
Maspero Nile Heights exhibits a commercial podium on the ground floor, FTTH Triple Play System, elevators, and a spacious garage. It is considered one of the best administrative projects in West El-Balad.

Cairo City Center
The project features a wide range of shops, retail outlets, dining venues, cafes, and recreational facilities. It is 6 minutes away from the Egyptian Museum. You can find elite retail units for sale in Maspero Mall, Downtown Cairo.

City Edge implemented a myriad of amenities in Maspero Business Tower to turn it into a one-of-a-kind work environment. They include firefighting systems, maintenance services, and the best security measures.

Things to Do & Places to Go in Downtown Cairo, Egypt
Discovering the rich history of Egypt is a must when in Downtown Cairo. The area hosts many iconic landmarks where you can have a blissful time, plus enrich your knowledge and indulge in artistry.
For instance, West El Balad exhibits:
The Egyptian Museum

If you are looking for a place where you can enjoy an exquisite shopping experience, Downtown Cairo, Egypt, features various retail outlets, such as:
Mad Stitches

Moreover, one of the best ways to explore the hidden gems of Downtown is on foot. West El Balad is a pedestrian-friendly area where you can wander and check its eateries, delightful shops, and vibrant boulevards.
Additionally, one of the must-visit attractions of West El-Balad is Cinema Radio, where the legendary Umm Kalthoum once sang. It also screened many of Egypt’s most prominent movies.
Discovering the classic architecture, lively cafes, and vibrant shops of Midan Falaki is a joyful experience too. Not to mention that Downtown Cairo, Egypt, is filled with souvenir shops where you can get your loved ones a distinctive gift.
